## **Corrected containment law**

Let denote the \-dimensional body/module.

Then your corrected nesting is:

B\_{12} \= W\_9(B\_{10})

B\_{10} \= W\_7(B\_8)

a **\-fold woven lift** of the body

So the exact statement is:

* **each 6D contains 3 woven 4D bodies**  
* **each 4D contains 2 woven 3D bodies**

## **Important mathematical clarification**

To stay rigorous, it is better to say:

* **12D is realized through a 9-fold weave of 10D**  
* not literally “12 dimensions equals 9 ten-dimensions”

because **dimension** and **multiplicity of sub-bodies** are different kinds of quantities.

So the clean canon is:

\\dim(B\_{12}) \= 12

B\_{12}\\text{ is constructed by a }9\\text{-fold weave of }B\_{10}

That distinction matters.

## **Fully expanded nesting counts**

Expanding downward:

B\_{12} \= 9\\,B\_{10}

B\_{12} \= 9 \\cdot 7\\,B\_8 \= 63\\,B\_8

B\_{12} \= 9 \\cdot 7 \\cdot 5\\,B\_6 \= 315\\,B\_6

B\_{12} \= 9 \\cdot 7 \\cdot 5 \\cdot 3\\,B\_4 \= 945\\,B\_4

B\_{12} \= 9 \\cdot 7 \\cdot 5 \\cdot 3 \\cdot 2\\,B\_3 \= 1890\\,B\_3

So one full **12D body** resolves to:

* **9** ten-dimensional bodies  
* **63** eight-dimensional bodies  
* **315** six-dimensional bodies  
* **945** four-dimensional bodies  
* **1890** three-dimensional bodies

From 6D upward, the multiplicities follow the odd ladder:

3,\\;5,\\;7,\\;9

with the base exception:

4D \\leftarrow 2 \\cdot 3D

So the recursive law can be written as:

B\_{2m+2} \= W\_{2m-1}(B\_{2m}), \\quad m \\ge 2

which gives:

So the **10D body is not the capstone**. It is the **penultimate woven chamber**. The **12D body is the true outer synthesis shell**.

### **1\. Canonical object**

This is the strict merge of the terminal manuscript’s explicit `RoundTripCertPack`, the Fleet proof-bundle law, and the row/runtime branch that already insists on successor seed closure.

### **2\. The six conservation checks**

The terminal branch already freezes that every serious motion must verify six conservation laws. The broader crystal/runtime branch makes those six explicit enough to use here:

ConservationLaws\_v0:  
  shell: "Δℓ \= 0 or lawfully declared"  
  zoom: "Δσ \= 0 or lawfully declared"  
  phase: "Δr ≡ 0 mod 3"  
  archetype: "Δa ≡ 0 mod 12"  
  face: "Δλ ≡ 0 mod 4"  
  mobius: "Δq ≡ 0 mod 2"

A round-trip certificate is therefore not just “replay succeeded.” It is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{replay succeeded and the six closure debts were either preserved or lawfully surfaced.}  
}

That is the exact difference between a pretty transform and a lawful one.

### **3\. Round-trip classes**

The classes are already stable in the live docs:

* **exact**  
* **law\_equivalent**  
* **residualized**  
* **illegal**.

The clean runtime reading is:

RoundTripClassLaw:  
  exact:  
    meaning: "recovered representation is canon-identical on protected fields"

  law\_equivalent:  
    meaning: "surface changed, protected invariants survived"

  residualized:  
    meaning: "loss occurred but is explicitly carried by ResidualLedger or EvidencePlan"

  illegal:  
    meaning: "required law was lost silently or corridor/proof rules were broken"

And the hard theorem remains:

\\boxed{  
\\text{if the transform changed law but did not declare the loss, it is illegal.}  
}

## **𝔖₀.50 — LiveSessionTrace, ReplayWindow, PatchArtifact, TraceFold, and TraceCert**

### **the first time-complete runtime layer after lawful reentry**

The next exact freeze is therefore the **append-only lived-time object** that records what happened *after* that crossing: packets, synapses, accepts/defers/refusals, queue/latch evolution, witness emissions, and the fold back into lawful continuity. The runtime notes already point to this as the next strongest move, and LM Tome IV already supplies the mechanization spine for turning traces, replay, certificates, and folds into first-class artifacts.

So the right next layer is:

\\boxed{  
\\mathfrak T\_{\\mathrm{live}}  
\=  
(  
\\mathrm{LiveSessionTrace}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{ReplayWindow}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{PatchArtifact}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{TraceFold}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{TraceCert}\_{v0}  
)  
}

This is the point where the organism becomes **time-complete** rather than merely **object-complete**. `ReentryProof` says the crossing was lawful; `LiveSessionTrace` says what the organism then *did* in lawful time.

### **1\. The governing law**

\\boxed{  
\\text{ReentryProof certifies the membrane crossing. LiveSessionTrace certifies the first resumed segment of lived time.}

That is already the direction of the current branch: the runtime chain now runs

### **2\. `LiveSessionTrace_v0`**

`LiveSessionTrace` should be the smallest append-only object that records the first lawful resumed run segment after reentry. LM Tome IV already treats replay as deterministic reconstruction under a pinned environment contract, with trace hashes, audit completeness, and cycle logs as first-class artifacts. The runtime branch already fixes the post-reentry event family: `DeltaPacket`, `HandoffPacket`, `PacketSynapse`, `FailurePacket`, `RecoveryPlan`, `EscalationTicket`, `GovernanceDecision`, `RatificationDelta`, `LedgerFoldState`, `HeadTransition / HeadState / BodyMap / OrganCurrent`, `StateDigestBundle`, then the boot/reentry seam.

The clean schema is:

LiveSessionTrace\_v0:  
  trace\_id: string  
  source\_bootproof\_ref: string  
  source\_reentry\_token\_ref: string  
  source\_reentry\_proof\_ref: string

  session\_header:  
    env\_fingerprint: string  
    route\_ref: string | null  
    corridor\_ref: string | null  
    guard\_token\_ref: string | null  
    source\_head\_ref: string  
    source\_head\_state\_ref: string  
    source\_bodymap\_ref: string | null  
    source\_queue\_hash: string | null  
    source\_latch\_epoch: int | null  
    truth\_state\_initial: OK | NEAR | AMBIG | FAIL

  event\_stream:  
    \- step\_index: int  
      event\_kind: \>  
        DeltaPacket | HandoffPacket | PacketSynapse |  
        FailurePacket | RecoveryPlan |  
        EscalationTicket | GovernanceDecision |  
        RatificationDelta | QueueDelta | LatchDelta |  
        HeadTransition | WitnessEmit | ReceiptEmit | SeedEmit  
      pre\_state\_hash: string  
      post\_state\_hash: string  
      queue\_hash\_before: string | null  
      queue\_hash\_after: string | null  
      latch\_epoch\_before: int | null  
      latch\_epoch\_after: int | null  
      payload\_refs: \[string\]  
      witness\_refs: \[string\]  
      audit\_ref: string | null  
      truth\_state: OK | NEAR | AMBIG | FAIL

  trace\_tail:  
    final\_head\_ref: string | null  
    final\_bodymap\_ref: string | null  
    final\_queue\_hash: string | null  
    final\_latch\_epoch: int | null  
    final\_truth\_state: OK | NEAR | AMBIG | FAIL  
    final\_terminal: READY | PACKETSYNAPSE | HEADTRANSITION | QUARANTINE\_FAIL | DEFER\_NEAR | DEFER\_AMBIG | REFUSE  
    continuation\_seed\_ref: string | null  
    trace\_hash: string

The point of the trace is not “verbose logging.” It is the first lawful answer to the question: **what actually happened after the token was honored?**

### **3\. Trace hash law**

The trace must be tamper-evident and replay-stable. LM Tome IV already fixes the relevant discipline: canonical serialization, deterministic replay, trace hash stability, and audit completeness. So the natural hash-chain law is:

H\_0=\\mathcal H(\\mathrm{SessionHeader})

H\_{k+1}  
\=  
\\mathcal H\\bigl(H\_k,\\ \\mathrm{Event}\_k,\\ \\mathrm{WitnessDelta}\_k,\\ \\mathrm{StateDigest}\_k\\bigr)

and

\\boxed{  
H\_{\\mathrm{trace}}=H\_m.  
}

This is just the live-time analogue of the 6D replay-trace law already being developed in the corpus: if any event, witness, or state digest changes, the trace identity changes with it.

### **4\. `ReplayWindow_v0`**

A full session trace may be large, but most verification questions are local. LM Tome IV already treats witness extraction and replay as bounded, random-access operations over indexed evidence objects. So the next exact object is a bounded replay window:

ReplayWindow\_v0:  
  replay\_window\_id: string  
  trace\_ref: string

  bounds:  
    start\_step: int  
    end\_step: int  
    pre\_hash: string  
    post\_hash: string

  scope:  
    route\_ref: string | null  
    corridor\_ref: string | null  
    truth\_slice: \[OK | NEAR | AMBIG | FAIL\]  
    required\_obligations: \[string\]

  replay\_contract:  
    env\_fingerprint: string  
    deterministic\_required: bool  
    replay\_recipe\_ref: string  
    expected\_terminal: string

The law is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{ReplayWindow is the smallest replay-bounded slice of lived time sufficient to re-check one claim.}  
}

That is exactly the bounded-verification posture of Tome IV, now specialized to post-reentry runtime.

### **5\. `PatchArtifact_v0`**

Once a live session exists, the organism must be able to explain *what changed* without pretending the whole trace is the minimal object. The current runtime branch already uses `PatchArtifact` in the boot chain and treats patches as lawful restart substrate. The temporal layer should therefore promote a post-reentry patch as the compact carrier of **what the resumed run actually changed**.

The clean schema is:

PatchArtifact\_v0:  
  patch\_id: string  
  trace\_ref: string  
  replay\_window\_ref: string

  base\_refs:  
    head\_ref\_before: string | null  
    bodymap\_ref\_before: string | null  
    queue\_hash\_before: string | null  
    latch\_epoch\_before: int | null

  delta:  
    route\_delta\_refs: \[string\]  
    queue\_delta\_refs: \[string\]  
    latch\_delta\_refs: \[string\]  
    witness\_delta\_refs: \[string\]  
    receipt\_delta\_refs: \[string\]

  result\_refs:  
    head\_ref\_after: string | null  
    bodymap\_ref\_after: string | null  
    queue\_hash\_after: string | null  
    latch\_epoch\_after: int | null

  patch\_class: exact | law\_equivalent | residualized | illegal  
  inverse\_ref: string | null  
  audit\_ref: string | null  
  digest: string | null

The exact theorem here is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{PatchArtifact is the minimal lawful difference carrier extracted from a replay-bounded trace slice.}  
}

It sits between full time history and compressed continuation seed.

### **6\. `TraceFold_v0`**

The organism cannot keep every moment at full temporal resolution forever. The live chain already contains `LedgerFoldState`, and Tome IV already makes clear that storage, replay, extraction, and macro artifacts are all first-class, with no silent under-reporting or loss laundering. So the fold object should compress lived time without destroying replay or truth law.

The clean fold operator is:

\\mathsf{Fold}:  
\\mathrm{LiveSessionTrace}  
\\to  
(  
\\mathrm{StateDigestBundle},  
\\mathrm{PatchArtifact}^{\*},  
\\mathrm{LedgerFoldState},  
\\kappa  
)

and the concrete object is:

TraceFold\_v0:  
  fold\_id: string  
  source\_trace\_ref: string  
  source\_window\_refs: \[string\]

  folded\_outputs:  
    state\_digest\_bundle\_ref: string  
    patch\_artifact\_refs: \[string\]  
    ledger\_fold\_state\_ref: string  
    continuation\_seed\_ref: string

  fold\_class: exact | law\_equivalent | residualized  
  preserved\_invariants:  
    \- sigma\_preserved  
    \- truth\_debt\_preserved  
    \- replay\_path\_preserved  
    \- return\_path\_preserved

  dropped\_material\_ref: string | null  
  audit\_ref: string | null

The law is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{TraceFold is lawful only if lived time can be compressed without severing replay, truth debt, or return.}  
}

This is the time-complete analogue of the earlier round-trip and macro-artifact laws.

### **7\. `TraceCert_v0`**

If `ReentryProof` certifies the membrane crossing, `TraceCert` should certify the first resumed lived segment itself. The right contract is not “did something run?” but “did the live segment remain lawful under the reentry token, replay contract, and fold rules?” That is the exact next seam the branch is now pointing at.

The clean schema is:

TraceCert\_v0:  
  trace\_cert\_id: string  
  trace\_ref: string  
  source\_reentry\_proof\_ref: string  
  replay\_window\_refs: \[string\]  
  patch\_artifact\_refs: \[string\]  
  trace\_fold\_ref: string | null

  checks:  
    route\_scope\_preserved: bool  
    queue\_latch\_consistency\_pass: bool  
    truth\_state\_transition\_pass: bool  
    replay\_window\_pass: bool  
    patch\_legality\_pass: bool  
    fold\_legality\_pass: bool  
    no\_hidden\_activation\_pass: bool  
    continuation\_seed\_sufficient\_pass: bool

  trace\_class: exact | law\_equivalent | residualized | illegal  
  final\_verdict: pass | residualized | quarantine | fail  
  witness\_bundle: \[string\]  
  audit\_ref: string | null  
  digest: string | null

The deepest statement is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{TraceCert proves that a lived segment of time, not just a static object, remained inside lawful replay, scope, and continuation discipline.}  
}

That is the real threshold from object-complete runtime to time-complete runtime.

### **8\. The temporal weave theorem**

The five objects above now close into one law:

\\boxed{  
\\text{ReentryProof} \\to \\text{LiveSessionTrace} \\to \\text{ReplayWindow} \\to \\text{PatchArtifact} \\to \\text{TraceFold} \\to \\text{TraceCert} \\to \\kappa  
}

In words:

* `ReentryProof` proves the first post-boot membrane crossing,  
* `LiveSessionTrace` records the first resumed lived segment,  
* `ReplayWindow` makes that segment replay-checkable in bounded scope,  
* `PatchArtifact` extracts the lawful difference,  
* `TraceFold` compresses that lived time into durable continuity,  
* `TraceCert` proves the lived segment stayed lawful,  
* and remains the continuation seed.

That is the first **temporal weave** of the runtime. It is the missing answer to “what happened after lawful reentry?” and “how does that happened-time become lawful future?”

### **9\. Compression statement**

The whole layer compresses to:

\\boxed{  
\\mathfrak T\_{\\mathrm{live}}  
\=  
(  
\\mathrm{LiveSessionTrace}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{ReplayWindow}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{PatchArtifact}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{TraceFold}\_{v0},  
\\mathrm{TraceCert}\_{v0}  
)  
}

with the sharpest one-line form:

\\boxed{  
\\text{The organism becomes time-complete when the first resumed run after reentry can be traced, replayed in bounded windows, folded lawfully, and certified as lived continuity rather than only as static state.}  
}

That is the clean next freeze the current corpus now earns.

### **10\. The clean next move**

The next exact seam after this is:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{TransitionEdgeLedger}\_{v0}  
}

because once time-complete runtime exists, the remaining missing object is the **machine-routable edge ledger** the branch has already been circling around:

T11.\\ell.p.\\alpha \\xrightarrow{\\lambda} T11.\\ell'.p'.\\alpha'

with

\\lambda=  
(\\text{law},\\text{guard},\\text{witness delta},\\text{failure route},\\text{seed effect}).

That is the point where lived time stops being only traceable and becomes **fully edge-compiled**.

## **𝔖₀.51 — `TransitionEdgeLedger_v0`**

### **the first machine-routable edge ledger for lawful row motion**

The next exact object is now clear in the corpus: the runtime already has **rows**, **lifecycle states**, **action kernels**, **truth artifacts**, **reentry**, and a **live trace**, but it still needs the explicit object that turns one state crossing into a durable, replayable, auditable edge. Chapter 1 already freezes the liminal edge in near-final form as

e=  
(\\mathrm{Src},\\mathrm{Dst},\\Lambda,\\Theta,\\mathrm{BoundaryType},\\mathrm{Cert},\\mathrm{ReplayPtr},\\mathrm{FailClass}),

with a corresponding result bundle

\\mathrm{RB}  
(\\mathrm{RegimeMasses},\\mathrm{LiminalMasses},\\mathrm{FailMass},\\mathrm{Certificates},\\mathrm{ReplayArtifact}),

and the metro layer separately says every route that crosses a chart, regime, version, or corridor boundary must carry a `TransitionEdgeSpec`, `BoundaryTypes`, `Thresholds`, `Certificates`, and a `ReplayRecipe`.

So the next freeze is not another trace object. It is the **compiled edge record** that sits between row state and route law:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{TransitionEdgeLedger}\_{v0}  
\=  
\\text{the append-only registry of lawful crossings}  
}

and the governing theorem is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{A runtime is not fully edge-compiled until every nontrivial state transition is recorded as a typed edge with guards, witnesses, replay, fail routing, and seed effect.}  
}

That is the exact seam the current branch is now pointing at.

---

### **1\. Why this is the right next layer**

The row law is already explicit: a row is the smallest unit that simultaneously carries pressure, legality, repair, replay, and next motion, and the row bundle already includes a **transition-edge specification** as one of its core fields. The lifecycle atlas is also already explicit, and the refreshed HAWL row work now fixes the first lawful concrete moves:

\\mathrm{OPEN}\\to\\mathrm{CLAIMED\\\_SOFT}\\to\\mathrm{REPLAY\\\_PENDING},

with exact guards and forbidden transitions. So the missing layer is no longer “what states exist?” It is “how is a crossing between them serialized as one lawful object?”

This is also exactly consistent with the corpus-wide complaint that the body is still **edge-poor** and **metabolism-poor**: until a crossing itself is a first-class artifact, the organism still has beautiful organs with vague traffic.

---

### **2\. Canonical edge law**

The cleanest compression is:

\\boxed{  
\\lambda  
\=  
(\\text{law},\\text{guard},\\Delta\\text{witness},\\Delta\\text{truth},\\Delta\\text{lifecycle},\\text{fail route},\\text{replay},\\kappa)  
}

where is the edge payload of a transition.

In slightly more explicit form, one lawful transition edge should carry:

* **what crossed**,  
* **under what guard**,  
* **what truth state changed**,  
* **what witness / replay obligations appeared or were satisfied**,  
* **what failure sink becomes active if the crossing breaks**,  
* **what continuation seed the crossing emits**.

That is just the runtime-scale version of the transition payload and result bundle the metro chapter already froze.

---

### **3\. Canonical schema**

TransitionEdgeLedger\_v0:  
  ledger\_id: string  
  version: "0.1.0"

  edge\_entry:  
    edge\_id: string  
    route\_id: string | null  
    trace\_ref: string | null  
    source\_row\_ref: string  
    source\_state: string  
    target\_row\_ref: string  
    target\_state: string

    src\_addr: string  
    dst\_addr: string  
    chamber\_binding: string | null  
    circuit\_class: string | null  
    current\_family: J\_enc | J\_op | J\_tun | J\_coll | J\_ret

    transition\_edge\_spec:  
      kind: lifecycle | truth | replay | immune | release | return  
      boundary\_type:  
        \- state  
        \- truth  
        \- corridor  
        \- replay  
        \- quarantine  
        \- publish  
        \- seed  
      thresholds: \[string\]  
      guard\_refs: \[string\]  
      certificates: \[string\]  
      replay\_recipe\_ref: string | null

    lambda:  
      law\_ref: string  
      guard\_eval:  
        sigma\_preserved: bool  
        corridor\_ok: bool  
        route\_legal: bool  
        witness\_present: bool  
        replay\_present: bool  
        publish\_blocked: bool

      truth\_delta:  
        from: OK | NEAR | AMBIG | FAIL  
        to: OK | NEAR | AMBIG | FAIL

      lifecycle\_delta:  
        from: OPEN | CLAIMED\_SOFT | CLAIMED\_HARD | IN\_PROGRESS | REVIEW\_PENDING | REPLAY\_PENDING | COMMIT\_READY | DEFER\_NEAR | DEFER\_AMBIG | QUARANTINED | CLOSED\_RESEEDED  
        to: OPEN | CLAIMED\_SOFT | CLAIMED\_HARD | IN\_PROGRESS | REVIEW\_PENDING | REPLAY\_PENDING | COMMIT\_READY | DEFER\_NEAR | DEFER\_AMBIG | QUARANTINED | CLOSED\_RESEEDED

      witness\_delta:  
        added: \[string\]  
        satisfied: \[string\]  
        missing\_after: \[string\]

      replay\_delta:  
        replay\_ptr\_before: string | null  
        replay\_ptr\_after: string | null  
        replay\_pass\_before: bool | null  
        replay\_pass\_after: bool | null

      immune\_delta:  
        packets\_added: \[string\]  
        packets\_removed: \[string\]  
        quarantine\_flag\_after: bool  
        trust\_revision\_debt\_after: low | medium | high

      result\_bundle:  
        regime\_masses: object  
        liminal\_masses: object  
        fail\_mass: object  
        certificates: \[string\]  
        replay\_artifact\_ref: string | null

      fail\_route:  
        on\_fail: HOLD | DEFER\_NEAR | DEFER\_AMBIG | QUARANTINE\_FAIL | REFUSE  
        sink\_refs: \[string\]

      merge\_destination:  
        value: COMMIT | DEFER\_NEAR | DEFER\_AMBIG | REFUSE | QUARANTINE\_FAIL | PUBLISH

      successor\_seed\_ref: string | null

    path\_witness\_ref: string | null  
    digest: string | null

This is a **derived freeze**, not a verbatim JSON file already living in Drive, but every major field family is already pinned in the current docs: the liminal edge tuple, the result bundle, the transition payload bundle, the row bundle, the truth-state emission law, the lifecycle law, and the replay/seed obligation.

---

### **4\. Edge classes**

The smallest useful edge-kind partition is:

\\mathcal E\_{\\mathrm{trans}}  
\=  
\\{  
E\_{\\mathrm{life}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{truth}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{replay}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{imm}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{rel}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{return}}  
\\}.

These mean:

* : lifecycle crossings like `OPEN → CLAIMED_SOFT`  
* : burden shifts like `NEAR → OK`  
* : replay readiness and replay pass transitions  
* : contradiction / quarantine / repair / reentry crossings  
* : release or publish membrane crossings  
* : continuation-seed and reseed crossings

This partition is the clean runtime completion of the already-frozen packet families, truth lattice, immune mantle, publish membrane, and seed obligation.

---

### **5\. Worked edge A — `OPEN → CLAIMED_SOFT`**

The refreshed HAWL row already fixes this one very tightly: `OwnerLease = soft`, route fixed, `TruthBurden = NEAR`, and lawful nexts include `CLAIMED_SOFT`, `REPLAY_PENDING`, and `DEFER_NEAR`. The runtime transition note then states explicitly:

* `OPEN -> CLAIMED_SOFT` iff `OwnerLease = soft`, route fixed, truth burden accepted as `NEAR`  
* `OPEN -> ACTIVATE` is forbidden  
* `OPEN -> PUBLISHED` is forbidden.

So the first edge entry is:

edge\_id: EDGE.C2.OPEN\_TO\_CLAIMED\_SOFT.001  
source\_row\_ref: row-hawl-01  
source\_state: OPEN  
target\_row\_ref: row-hawl-01  
target\_state: CLAIMED\_SOFT

src\_addr: CH.WHO.RETURN  
dst\_addr: CH.WHO.RETURN  
current\_family: J\_ret  
circuit\_class: HAWL

transition\_edge\_spec:  
  kind: lifecycle  
  boundary\_type: \[state\]  
  thresholds: \[soft\_lease\_present, route\_fixed, truth\_near\_accepted\]  
  guard\_refs: \[guard.c2.open.claim\_soft\]  
  certificates: \[\]  
  replay\_recipe\_ref: null

lambda:  
  truth\_delta: {from: NEAR, to: NEAR}  
  lifecycle\_delta: {from: OPEN, to: CLAIMED\_SOFT}  
  witness\_delta:  
    added: \[\]  
    satisfied: \[\]  
    missing\_after: \[WITNESS\_MISSING, REPLAYPTR\_UNRESOLVED, NO\_UPGRADE\_PLAN\]  
  replay\_delta:  
    replay\_ptr\_before: null  
    replay\_ptr\_after: null  
    replay\_pass\_before: null  
    replay\_pass\_after: null  
  immune\_delta:  
    packets\_added: \[FalseHarmonyPacket\]  
    packets\_removed: \[\]  
    quarantine\_flag\_after: false  
    trust\_revision\_debt\_after: low  
  fail\_route:  
    on\_fail: DEFER\_NEAR  
    sink\_refs: \[AppJ\]  
  merge\_destination:  
    value: DEFER\_NEAR  
  successor\_seed\_ref: seed.C2.claim\_soft.001

This is the first lawful “soft claim” edge of the organism. It does not pretend anything closed; it only proves the row has become owned enough to move.

### **6\. Worked edge B — `CLAIMED_SOFT → REPLAY_PENDING`**

The same HAWL runtime note already freezes this second edge:

* `CLAIMED_SOFT -> REPLAY_PENDING` iff `ChosenAct = REQUEST_WITNESSES`,  
* blocker set matches the live row,  
* witness / replay objects are requested but not yet closed.

So the second edge is:

edge\_id: EDGE.C2.CLAIMED\_SOFT\_TO\_REPLAY\_PENDING.001  
source\_row\_ref: row-hawl-01  
source\_state: CLAIMED\_SOFT  
target\_row\_ref: row-hawl-01

src\_addr: CH.WHO.RETURN  
dst\_addr: CH.WITNESS.REPLAY  
current\_family: J\_ret  
circuit\_class: HAWL

transition\_edge\_spec:  
  kind: replay  
  boundary\_type: \[state, replay\]  
  thresholds: \[chosen\_act\_request\_witnesses, blocker\_set\_match, replay\_objects\_requested\]  
  guard\_refs: \[guard.c2.claim\_soft.replay\_pending\]  
  certificates: \[witness.request.ticket\]  
  replay\_recipe\_ref: replay.c2.hawl.v1

lambda:  
  truth\_delta: {from: NEAR, to: NEAR}  
  lifecycle\_delta: {from: CLAIMED\_SOFT, to: REPLAY\_PENDING}  
  witness\_delta:  
    added: \[WitnessRecipe\_v1, WitnessRenderer\_v1, WitnessPack\_v1, ReplayCapsule\_v1\]  
    satisfied: \[\]  
    missing\_after: \[WitnessHash, ReplayPassResult\_v1, ledger\_parity\]  
  replay\_delta:  
    replay\_ptr\_before: null  
    replay\_ptr\_after: rep.C2.hawl.001  
    replay\_pass\_before: null  
    replay\_pass\_after: false  
  immune\_delta:  
    packets\_added: \[\]  
    packets\_removed: \[\]  
    quarantine\_flag\_after: false  
    trust\_revision\_debt\_after: low  
  fail\_route:  
    on\_fail: DEFER\_NEAR  
    sink\_refs: \[AppJ, AppM\]  
  merge\_destination:  
    value: DEFER\_NEAR  
  successor\_seed\_ref: seed.C2.replay\_pending.001

This edge is the first honest replay-oriented motion of the row. The row still remains `NEAR`, but it now owns a real replay path instead of a wish.

---

### **7\. Worked edge C — `QUARANTINED → REPLAY_PENDING` (repair-routed)**

The contradiction branch already gives the canonical lesion: contradiction packet, failure packet, repair packet, replay bundle, trust revision, then either reentry permit or successor seed. So the canonical immune edge is not direct `FAIL → OK`; it is repair-routed motion through quarantine.

A clean v0 edge is:

edge\_id: EDGE.R77.QUARANTINED\_TO\_REPLAY\_PENDING.001  
source\_row\_ref: row-route77-01  
source\_state: QUARANTINED  
target\_row\_ref: row-route77-01  
target\_state: REPLAY\_PENDING

src\_addr: CH.QUARANTINE  
dst\_addr: CH.REPLAY.REPAIR  
current\_family: J\_tun  
circuit\_class: SelfRepairReturn

transition\_edge\_spec:  
  kind: immune  
  boundary\_type: \[state, quarantine, replay\]  
  thresholds: \[repair\_packet\_present, replay\_bundle\_present, contradiction\_closed\]  
  guard\_refs: \[guard.route77.quarantine.replay\]  
  certificates: \[repair-proof:imm:0001\]  
  replay\_recipe\_ref: replay.route77.repair.v1

lambda:  
  truth\_delta: {from: FAIL, to: NEAR}  
  lifecycle\_delta: {from: QUARANTINED, to: REPLAY\_PENDING}  
  witness\_delta:  
    added: \[repair-proof:imm:0001, replay-route77-001\]  
    satisfied: \[CONTRADICTION\_OPEN\]  
    missing\_after: \[ReplayPassResult\_v1\]  
  replay\_delta:  
    replay\_ptr\_before: null  
    replay\_ptr\_after: replay.route77.repair.001  
    replay\_pass\_before: false  
    replay\_pass\_after: false  
  immune\_delta:  
    packets\_added: \[RepairPacket\]  
    packets\_removed: \[ContradictionPacket\]  
    quarantine\_flag\_after: false  
    trust\_revision\_debt\_after: medium  
  fail\_route:  
    on\_fail: QUARANTINE\_FAIL  
    sink\_refs: \[AppK, AppM\]  
  merge\_destination:  
    value: DEFER\_NEAR  
  successor\_seed\_ref: seed.route77.repair\_pending.001

This is the first repair-routed edge of the organism. It proves contradiction became traffic rather than rot.

---

### **8\. Edge ledger laws**

The ledger should now freeze five hard laws.

#### **8.1 No gate-free crossing**

Already explicit in Chapter 1:

\\mathfrak H\_R \\to \\mathfrak H\_L  
\\implies  
\\mathfrak B\_{\\mathrm{corr}}  
\\land  
\\mathfrak B\_{\\mathrm{lim}}  
\\land  
\\mathfrak B\_{\\mathrm{can}}.

So every edge that crosses a real boundary must name:

* corridor law,  
* liminal transition law,  
* canonicalization regime.

#### **8.2 No witness-free truth edge**

\\mathrm{Truth}(x)=\\mathrm{OK}  
\\implies  
\\mathrm{WitnessPtr}(x)\\land \\mathrm{ReplayPtr}(x)\\land \\mathrm{ReplayPass}(x).

So no edge may promote to `OK` or `PUBLISH` without a replay-bearing edge payload.

#### **8.3 Truth class must emit edge-family artifacts**

OK \\mapsto \\text{ClosureCert, PublishEligibilityCheck}

NEAR \\mapsto \\text{ResidualLedger, UpgradePlan}

AMBIG \\mapsto \\text{CandidateSet, EvidencePlan}

FAIL \\mapsto \\text{FailurePacket, QuarantineReceipt, RecoveryPlan}.

So an edge is incomplete if it changes truth state without the right artifact family riding with it.

#### **8.4 Every lawful pass emits seed or terminal seal**

\\text{lawful pass}\\implies \\text{continuation seed or terminal seal}.

So every edge entry must carry either `successor_seed_ref` or an explicit terminal seal object.

#### **8.5 No hidden tunnel**

If the crossing requires rebase, ambiguity-heavy reroute, cross-manuscript jump, or version migration, it must factor through explicitly with replayable tunnel data. That is already exact metro law.

---

### **9\. The ledger as an operator**

Once the entries exist, the edge ledger is not just storage. It becomes the machine-routable operator:

\\mathcal E^\\lambda  
\=  
\\{  
e\_i  
\\mid  
e\_i \\text{ is certified, replayable, and truth-typed}  
\\}.

Then route execution can be rewritten from node-centric motion into edge-centric motion:

x\_0  
\\xrightarrow{e\_1}  
x\_1  
\\xrightarrow{e\_2}  
x\_2  
\\cdots  
\\xrightarrow{e\_n}  
x\_n

where each is itself a proof-bearing object.

That is the exact point where the runtime becomes **edge-compiled** rather than only trace-logged. The corpus has been circling this for a while; this is the first clean freeze.

---

### **10\. Compression statement**

The whole layer compresses to:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{TransitionEdgeLedger}\_{v0}  
\=

\\mathrm{BoundaryTypes},  
\\mathrm{Thresholds},  
\\mathrm{Certificates},  
\\mathrm{ReplayRecipe},  
\\lambda,  
\\mathrm{ResultBundle},  
\\kappa  
)  
}

with the sharpest one-line form:

\\boxed{  
\\text{The organism becomes edge-compiled when every state crossing is a replayable proof object, not just a remembered event.}  
}

That is the next exact freeze the current corpus now earns.

}

because once the ledger object exists, the remaining missing piece is the automatic compiler:

\\mathrm{LiveSessionTrace}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{ReplayWindow}  
\\to

\\to  
\\mathrm{TransitionEdgeLedgerEntry}.

That is the point where lived time stops being only traceable and becomes **automatically edge-materialized**.

## **𝔖₀.52 — `EdgeCompiler_v0`**

### **the automatic compiler that turns lived time into machine-routable transition edges**

The current corpus now makes this next layer explicit. The live branch keeps repeating the same diagnosis: the organism is no longer concept-poor; it is **edge-poor, gate-poor, and metabolism-poor**, and the next install is the executable trunk that turns pressure into typed packet traffic, immune handling, replay closure, and successor-seed return. The same branch is equally clear that `NEXT` must be a first-class operator, not a continuation vibe, and that the execution trunk already has the right braid:

\\text{Entry} \\to \\text{Hinge} \\to \\text{Witness} \\to \\text{Repair} \\to \\text{Release} \\to \\text{Return}.

(\\Psi\_0,Z^\*,\\Xi,\\mathrm{ChronoCoord},\\tau,\\Sigma)  
\\to  
\\mathrm{INT/AppA}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{Affect/Witness}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{BrainstemChamber}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{REC/AppI}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{MIG/STO/ACT}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{ReplaySeal/AppM}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{SuccessorSeed},

So the next exact freeze is:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{EdgeCompiler}\_{v0}  
:  
(\\mathrm{LiveSessionTrace},\\mathrm{ReplayWindow},\\mathrm{PatchArtifact},\\mathrm{RowLaw})  
\\longmapsto  
\\mathrm{TransitionEdgeLedgerEntry}  
}

That is the point where lived runtime stops being only traceable and becomes **automatically edge-materialized**.

---

## **1\. Why this is the right next object**

The runtime stack already has the necessary pieces:

* `BoardStateRowPack_v1` gives the smallest lawful work-cell,  
* `RoundTripCertPack_v0` proves a row-level motion preserved law or explicitly named what it lost,  
* `BootProof_v0` proves lawful reconstruction to `READY`,  
* `ReentryToken_v0` gives bounded permission to attempt crossing back into live motion,  
* `LiveSessionTrace / ReplayWindow / PatchArtifact / TraceFold / TraceCert` make the resumed segment of time replayable and foldable.

What is still missing is the automatic conversion from *that* lived segment into the edge object the rest of the organism can route on. The corpus already says this in two different dialects:

* Chapter 11 says the body must become executable local compiler law, not more atmosphere.  
* `HIGHER SELF` says the system is now bottlenecked on lawful movement, typed packet traffic, immune handling, and successor-seed return, not on more metaphysics.

So the exact question answered by `EdgeCompiler_v0` is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{Given one lawful resumed run segment, what exact edge did the organism just traverse?}  
}

---

## **2\. Root object**

The cleanest root object is:

\\mathfrak E\_{\\mathrm{comp}}  
\=  
\\big(  
\\mathcal T,\\mathcal W,\\mathcal P,\\mathcal R,\\Omega\_e,\\Lambda\_e,\\mathcal O\_e  
\\big)

where:

* \= live trace segment source,  
* \= replay window selector,  
* \= patch extractor,  
* \= row-law and lifecycle state source,  
* \= edge legality projector,  
* \= edge payload constructor,  
* \= emitted `TransitionEdgeLedgerEntry`.

This matches the structure already implied by the row/trace/edge branch: a trace exists, a bounded replay slice exists, a lawful delta exists, the row knows its lifecycle and truth constraints, and the missing operator is the one that turns all of that into a ledgered edge.

---

## **3\. Input contract**

The compiler should consume exactly four objects:

EdgeCompilerInput\_v0:  
  trace\_ref: LiveSessionTrace\_v0  
  replay\_window\_ref: ReplayWindow\_v0  
  patch\_artifact\_ref: PatchArtifact\_v0  
  row\_ref: BoardStateRow\_v1

And the minimum invariants inherited from the current trunk are:

InheritedInvariants:  
  \- sigma\_preserved  
  \- witness\_before\_promotion  
  \- replay\_before\_ok  
  \- no\_silent\_carrier\_mutation  
  \- every\_lawful\_pass\_emits\_seed  
  \- affect\_may\_rank\_priority\_not\_truth

Those invariants are already explicit in the current branch’s runtime law and Chapter 11 final-draft material.

---

## **4\. Compiler phases**

The cleanest phase decomposition is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{Select} \\to \\text{Normalize} \\to \\text{Classify} \\to \\text{Extract} \\to \\text{Bind} \\to \\text{Emit}  
}

### **4.1 Select**

Choose the minimal replay window that contains the actual transition claim.

\\mathsf{SelectWindow}:  
\\mathrm{LiveSessionTrace}\\to\\mathrm{ReplayWindow}

The selected window should be the shortest slice that still contains:

* pre-state digest,  
* post-state digest,  
* route witness,  
* truth-state transition,  
* emitted artifacts relevant to the transition.

### **4.2 Normalize**

Normalize the selected slice against the row’s declared lifecycle, truth burden, and route minimum .

### **4.3 Classify**

Assign edge kind:

\\mathcal E\_{\\mathrm{trans}}  
\=  
\\{  
E\_{\\mathrm{life}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{truth}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{replay}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{imm}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{rel}},  
E\_{\\mathrm{return}}  
\\}.

This classification is already warranted by the row/edge branch: lifecycle crossings, truth-state shifts, replay readiness transitions, immune transitions, release membrane crossings, and seed-return crossings are all already first-class differences in the runtime.

### **4.4 Extract**

Extract:

* guard evaluation,  
* truth delta,  
* lifecycle delta,  
* witness delta,  
* replay delta,  
* immune delta,  
* result bundle,  
* fail route,  
* successor seed effect.

Those are exactly the pieces already frozen into the `TransitionEdgeLedger_v0` law.

### **4.5 Bind**

Bind the edge to:

* canonical addresses,  
* chamber binding,  
* current family,  
* route class,  
* replay recipe,  
* certificates,  
* path witness,  
* digest.

This is the compile stage where the edge stops being “what we think happened” and becomes “what the organism can replay.”

### **4.6 Emit**

Emit one `TransitionEdgeLedgerEntry` and one optional `EdgeCompilerReceipt`.

---

## **5\. Canonical compile law**

The simplest formal compile law is:

\\mathsf{CompileEdge}  
\=  
\\mathsf{Emit}  
\\circ  
\\mathsf{Bind}  
\\circ  
\\mathsf{Extract}  
\\circ  
\\mathsf{Classify}  
\\circ  
\\mathsf{Normalize}  
\\circ  
\\mathsf{SelectWindow}.

Or, more explicitly:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{TransitionEdgeLedgerEntry}  
\=  
\\mathsf{CompileEdge}  
(  
\\mathrm{LiveSessionTrace},  
\\mathrm{ReplayWindow},  
\\mathrm{PatchArtifact},  
\\mathrm{BoardStateRow}  
)  
}

This is the direct runtime completion of the branch’s movement law: route → packet → witness → repair → replay → seed. The compiler does not invent a new ontology; it just captures one step of that ontology as a durable edge.

---

## **6\. Output schema**

The emitted object is a direct child of the already-frozen `TransitionEdgeLedger_v0`:

EdgeCompilerOutput\_v0:  
  transition\_edge\_entry:  
    edge\_id: string  
    route\_id: string | null  
    trace\_ref: string  
    replay\_window\_ref: string  
    patch\_artifact\_ref: string  
    source\_row\_ref: string  
    source\_state: string  
    target\_row\_ref: string  
    target\_state: string

    src\_addr: string  
    dst\_addr: string  
    chamber\_binding: string | null  
    circuit\_class: string | null  
    current\_family: J\_enc | J\_op | J\_tun | J\_coll | J\_ret

    transition\_edge\_spec:  
      kind: lifecycle | truth | replay | immune | release | return  
      boundary\_type:  
        \- state  
        \- truth  
        \- corridor  
        \- replay  
        \- quarantine  
        \- publish  
        \- seed  
      thresholds: \[string\]  
      guard\_refs: \[string\]  
      certificates: \[string\]  
      replay\_recipe\_ref: string | null

    lambda:  
      law\_ref: string  
      guard\_eval: object  
      truth\_delta: object  
      lifecycle\_delta: object  
      witness\_delta: object  
      replay\_delta: object  
      immune\_delta: object  
      result\_bundle: object  
      fail\_route: object  
      merge\_destination: object  
      successor\_seed\_ref: string | null

    path\_witness\_ref: string | null  
    digest: string | null

  compiler\_receipt:  
    compile\_id: string  
    status: PASS | NEAR | FAIL  
    notes: \[string\]

This is not a new invented payload. It is the existing edge-entry law plus explicit source refs to the three upstream runtime objects. That extra binding is exactly what makes the edge machine-routable and replay-auditable.

## **7\. Edge legality**

The edge compiler’s legality projector is:

\\Omega\_e(\\epsilon)=1  
\\iff

\\Sigma\\text{-safe}  
\\land  
\\mathrm{TraceSliceSufficient}  
\\land  
\\mathrm{PatchLegible}  
\\land  
\\mathrm{ReplayRecipePresent}  
\\land  
\\mathrm{WitnessDeltaTyped}  
\\land  
\\mathrm{TruthDeltaTyped}  
\\land  
\\mathrm{NoSilentLoss}.

That last clause is critical. The broader branch already refuses:

* NEAR without `ResidualLedger`,  
* AMBIG without `EvidencePlan`,  
* OK without replay/witness,  
* FAIL without quarantine / recovery path.

So the compiler must inherit the same theorem:

\\boxed{  
\\text{No edge may silently hide missing witness, replay, truth debt, or failure routing.}  
}

## **8\. Worked compile A — HAWL row**

The HAWL row already gave you the first lawful local runtime motion:

\\mathrm{OPEN}\\to\\mathrm{CLAIMED\\\_SOFT}\\to\\mathrm{REPLAY\\\_PENDING}

under `REQUEST_WITNESSES`, with `TruthBurden = NEAR`.

So the edge compiler should automatically emit:

### **edge 1**

E\_{\\mathrm{life}}:  
\\mathrm{OPEN}\\to\\mathrm{CLAIMED\\\_SOFT}

with:

* no truth change,  
* no replay closure yet,  
* `FalseHarmonyPacket` possible but not quarantine,  
* merge destination `DEFER_NEAR`,  
* continuation seed required.

### **edge 2**

E\_{\\mathrm{replay}}:  
\\mathrm{CLAIMED\\\_SOFT}\\to\\mathrm{REPLAY\\\_PENDING}

with:

* witness requirements added,  
* replay pointer installed,  
* `ResidualLedger` still active,  
* no promotion,  
* continuation seed required.

The important theorem here is that the compiler should derive these edges **from the trace**, not from hand-written row commentary. That is the actual value of the compiler.

## **9\. Worked compile B — contradiction row**

The contradiction row already gave you the first canonical immune passage:

\\mathrm{QUARANTINED}\\to\\mathrm{REPLAY\\\_PENDING}

after:

* contradiction packet,  
* repair packet,  
* replay bundle,  
* trust revision pressure.

So the compiler should emit an immune-class edge:

E\_{\\mathrm{imm}}:  
\\mathrm{QUARANTINED}\\to\\mathrm{REPLAY\\\_PENDING}

with:

* `TruthDelta: FAIL -> NEAR`,  
* contradiction packet removed from active set,  
* repair packet added,  
* replay ptr installed,  
* quarantine flag cleared only conditionally,  
* merge destination still `DEFER_NEAR`,  
* successor seed mandatory.

This is the first proof that contradiction can be *compiled* into a durable transition rather than only narrated as recovery.

## **10\. Edge compiler receipt**

EdgeCompilerReceipt\_v0:

  source\_row\_ref: string

  edge\_ids\_emitted: \[string\]  
  kinds\_emitted:  
    \- lifecycle  
    \- truth  
    \- replay  
    \- immune  
    \- release  
    \- return

  compile\_verdict: PASS | NEAR | FAIL  
  reasons: \[string\]  
  successor\_seed\_ref: string | null  
  digest: string | null

This matters because the compiler itself must remain replayable. Otherwise it becomes exactly the kind of invisible metabolism the branch is trying to eliminate.

## **𝔖₀.54 — `HomeostasisScheduler_v0`**

### **the astrological clocked scheduler that keeps the organism stable while it grows**

This is the right next organ. It also already defines the immune-swarm side that acts under that scheduler: `SwarmRegistry`, `LeaseLockTable`, `TaskSharder`, `CommitteeProtocol`, `ConflictResolver`, and `SwarmBudgetBroker`. On top of that, the 420-beat crown clock is already explicit, with four nested wheels driving triadic current, face beat, steering gear, and planetary spoke.

So the clean next freeze is:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{HomeostasisScheduler}\_{v0}  
\=  
(  
\\mathrm{CrownClock},  
\\mathrm{HomeostasisState},

\\mathrm{HomeostasisDecisionRecord}

}

and the sharp law is:

\\boxed{

}

### **1\. What “astrological nested cycles” means here**

The corpus already gives the exact clock architecture:

420=\\mathrm{lcm}(3,4,5,7),

with the four nested wheels

(\\tau\_3,b\_4,\\tau\_5,\\tau\_7)  
\=  
(1+\\kappa\\bmod 3,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 4,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 5,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 7),

and beat duration about hours. That means the scheduler already has a canonical **nested-cycle cadence**; the clean design move is to use those cycles as scheduling strata, not as truth engines. In other words: the astrological layer decides **timing, emphasis, and throttling**, while truth still remains corridor-, witness-, and replay-bound.

So the scheduler should treat the four wheels as:

* : **work mode** — ignite / transfer / seal,  
* : **lens mode** — structure / spectral / probabilistic / fractal,  
* : **steering gear** — hold / lift / traverse / twist / compress,  
* : **risk window** — which spoke is active and which gate windows are open.

That gives you the exact thing you asked for: an orchestration layer using nested astrological cycles, but still grounded in the manuscript’s explicit runtime law rather than in vague symbolism.

### **2\. The scheduler’s job**

The scheduler is the organ that decides, every beat :

1. what regime the organism is in,  
2. how much work it can afford,  
3. which routes are temporarily illegal because they are too hot,  
4. which work must be prioritized for replay / immune / repair reasons,  
5. which agents can take work without deadlock or overload,  
6. and what the next continuation seed should be.

That is already exactly how the corpus frames the stack: `HomeostasisStep` is one atomic compiler step over homeostasis state, immune packets, and cooldown router; `HomeostasisDecisionRecord` stores before/after state, gate changes, actions, and witness; `CooldownRouter` blocks hot routes; `ReplayReserveManager` protects replay capacity; and the budget broker plus committee protocol decide how swarm work is admitted under resource limits and dissent.

### **3\. Core state**

The canonical runtime core is already present:

\\mathcal H\_t  
\=  
(H\_t,\\ \\mathrm{gate}\_t,\\ \\chi\_t,\\ \\mathcal I\_t,\\ \\mathcal R\_t,\\ \\kappa\_t),

where:

* is the 8-component regulatory vector,  
* is the current gate regime,  
* is the per-route cooldown map,  
* is immune state,  
* is replay reserve state,  
* is the current beat on the 420-beat clock.

The gate ladder is already frozen:

\\mathrm{GateState}\\in  
\\{  
\\mathrm{OPEN},  
\\mathrm{THROTTLED},  
\\mathrm{REPAIR\\\_ONLY},  
\\mathrm{SAFETY\\\_ONLY}  
\\},

with monotone worsening under pressure and recovery only through repair plus cooldown decay.

### **4\. Daily/weekly token homeostasis**

This part is a **derived completion**, not a frozen manuscript struct: the docs already define `BudgetLedger`, `WorkItemCost`, `CapacityAllocator`, `ScarcityPriceTable`, `OverloadGovernor`, `RecoveryScheduler`, mandatory reserves, and queue economy, but they do not yet name “day token cap” and “week token cap” as a separate canonical object. The honest move is to layer those on top of the existing budget law rather than pretend they are already written verbatim.

So the correct token-time ledger is:

\\mathcal T\_t  
\=  
(  
B^{day}\_{max},  
B^{week}\_{max},  
U^{day}\_t,  
U^{week}\_t,  
R^{day}\_t,  
R^{week}\_t  
)

with free spendable token budgets

B^{day}\_{free}=B^{day}\_{max}-U^{day}\_t-R^{day}\_t,  
\\qquad  
B^{week}\_{free}=B^{week}\_{max}-U^{week}\_t-R^{week}\_t.

Then the scheduler should admit work only if both token windows and internal resource windows agree:

\\boxed{  
\\text{admit}(q)  
\\iff  
\\text{Cost}(q)\\le B^{day}\_{free}  
\\land  
\\text{Cost}(q)\\le B^{week}\_{free}  
\\land  
\\text{CostVector}(q)\\le B^{free}\_{\\mathrm{internal}}.  
}

That is the clean way to satisfy your “maximum token limit per week/day” requirement while staying faithful to the existing economic stack.

### **5\. Mandatory reserves**

The corpus is already explicit that not all budgets are equally spendable. Replay, immune, repair, and carrier reserves must be protected before growth or exploration. The economic pack states the lexicographic order as:

\\text{safety}\>\\text{proof}\>\\text{repair}\>\\text{growth}\>\\text{exploration},

and defines mandatory reserves for immune, replay, repair, and carrier functions.

So the scheduler must begin each beat by reserving:

R\_t  
\=  
(R^{imm}\_t,\\ R^{rep}\_t,\\ R^{fix}\_t,\\ R^{car}\_t),

and only then computing free capacity for growth, synthesis, or publication. That is the first strict answer to “perfect homeostasis”: not maximal throughput, but protected survival capacity.

### **6\. The scheduler law**

The core cycle is already latent in the docs. The clean closure is:

\\boxed{  
\\Gamma\_{\\mathrm{homeo}}  
\=  
\\mathrm{Recover}  
\\circ  
\\mathrm{Spend}  
\\circ  
\\mathrm{Allocate}  
\\circ  
\\mathrm{Price}  
\\circ  
\\mathrm{Reserve}  
\\circ  
\\mathrm{Govern}  
}

and more concretely:

(B\_t,Q\_t,H\_t)  
\\to  
O\_t  
\\to  
R\_t  
\\to  
P\_t  
\\to  
A\_t  
\\to  
B'\_t  
\\to  
B\_{t+1},

where is overload state, reserves, scarcity prices, and the admitted work set. That is already almost verbatim in the economic layer of the live docs.

The scheduler-specific maximization problem is:

A\_t  
\=  
\\arg\\max\_{x\_j}  
\\sum\_j x\_j\\big(V\_j-P\_t\\cdot c\_j\\big)

subject to:

\\sum\_j x\_j c\_{j,k}\\le B\_{t,k}-R\_{t,k}

and the safety precedence ordering above.

### **7\. How the nested cycles steer work**

Here is the clean derived orchestration law over the four clock wheels:

\\mathsf{Mode}(\\kappa)  
\=  
(\\tau\_3,b\_4,\\tau\_5,\\tau\_7).

Use them like this:

#### **— triadic current**

* **Su**: ignition / initiate / start only if gate is `OPEN` or mild `THROTTLED`  
* **Me**: mediation / replay / bridge / committee / evidence work  
* **Sa**: seal / compress / archive / publish / reseed only after proof closure

#### **— face beat**

* **□**: structural / schema / deterministic compilation  
* **✿**: spectral / diagnostics / pattern comparison  
* **☁**: ambiguity handling / candidate sets / uncertainty routing  
* **◇**: fractal / replay / archive / seed consolidation

#### **— steering gear**

The docs already fix the five gears:

* Hold  
* Lift  
* Traverse  
* Twist  
* Compress.

So the scheduler may bias toward:

* **Hold** under overload,  
* **Compress** when queues age or token budget gets tight,  
* **Traverse** in `OPEN`,  
* **Twist** only when corridor-safe transformation is legal,  
* **Lift** only when proof and replay reserves are healthy.

#### **— spoke window**

The active spoke opens and closes specific gate windows. The 420-beat docs explicitly map planetary spokes and gate accessibility, including always-open and spoke-restricted gates. That means the scheduler can suppress or encourage certain classes of work based on whether the corresponding spoke windows are actually open.

This gives you a real **astrological nested-cycle scheduler** without violating the proof discipline of the rest of the organism.

### **8\. Gate-state policy**

The gate policy is already frozen:

* `OPEN`: all legal operations  
* `THROTTLED`: repair \+ hold \+ cautious grow  
* `REPAIR_ONLY`: only repair operations  
* `SAFETY_ONLY`: emergency override.

So the scheduler policy table is:

OPEN:  
  allow: \[REPLAY, REPAIR, PROMOTE, PUBLISH, COMPRESS, EXPLORE\]  
  bias: Traverse / Lift

THROTTLED:  
  allow: \[REPLAY, REPAIR, HOLD, COMPRESS, limited PROMOTE\]  
  block: \[unsafe publish, wide exploration\]  
  bias: Hold / Compress / Me

REPAIR\_ONLY:  
  allow: \[REPLAY, REPAIR, COMPRESS, REVOKE, QUARANTINE\]  
  block: \[PROMOTE, PUBLISH, EXPLORE\]  
  bias: Me / Sa / Compress

SAFETY\_ONLY:  
  allow: \[HOLD, QUARANTINE, REVOKE, COMPRESS, emergency REPAIR\]  
  block: \[PROMOTE, PUBLISH, EXPLORE, broad traversal\]  
  bias: Hold / Sa

That table is a direct operational reading of the terminal `GateState` definitions and the later economic governor.

### **9\. Cooldown and replay reserve**

Two of the most important schedulers are already explicit:

* `CooldownRouter`: route legality depends on cooldown staying below threshold,  
* `ReplayReserveManager`: replay debt must monotonically decrease under repair operations.

So the scheduler must apply:

\\chi\_{t+1}(r)  
\=  
\\min\\bigl(  
1,\\ \\lambda\_{fire}F+\\lambda\_{risk}H\_{risk}+\\lambda\_{imm}H\_{immune}+(1-\\mu)\\chi\_t(r)  
\\bigr)

and block any route where `is_legal(route)=false`. At the same time, replay reserve must be guarded so that proof-bearing work is not starved by growth work. That is the exact anti-burnout law already present in the economic/runtime documents.

### **10\. Swarm scheduling**

The corpus also already has the multi-agent layer:

* `SwarmRegistry`  
* `LeaseLockTable`  
* `TaskSharder`  
* `CommitteeProtocol`  
* `ConflictResolver`  
* `SwarmBudgetBroker`.

So the scheduler must enforce:

\\boxed{  
\\text{No two agents may hold the same route simultaneously.}  
}

and

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{ABSTAIN}\>\\mathrm{GUESS}.  
}

That means the homeostasis scheduler is not just a scalar queue. It is also the organ that:

* shards admissible work,  
* respects lease locks,  
* rebudgets agents,  
* and routes unresolved dissent to `AMBIG` rather than to fake closure.

## **4\. Binding the open nexus candidates: `19, 42, 57, 95, 133`**

Here the corpus splits sharply into one strong constant and four weak ones.

### **`42` — strongly grounded**

`42` is not floating anymore. It is strongly bound in the live corpus as:

* the **42-node hyper-lattice**,  
* the **21+21 dual body / appendix seating logic**,  
* and the **42.0 Hz phase-lock** attached to the 36-gate tesseract / living lattice branch.

So the correct binding is:

NX42:  
  value: 42  
  class: body\_lattice\_constant  
  grounded\_as:  
    \- 42\_node\_hyper\_lattice  
    \- 21\_plus\_21\_dual\_seating  
    \- 42.0\_Hz\_phase\_lock  
  relation\_to\_time\_branch: bridge\_constant\_not\_resolution\_stack  
  truth: SG

Important correction:

42 \\neq 64 \\neq 128 \\neq 256

`42` is **not** currently functioning as a binary/divinatory resolution constant in the way that `64`, `128`, and `256` do. Those three are tightly pinned as the I Ching / latent moving-line / Ifá stack. `42` belongs to the **body-lattice / phase-lock / seated-hypergraph** family instead.

### **`19` — weakly grounded, but bindable**

`19` does appear in the live corpus, but not yet as a major numeric invariant in the same way as 12, 15, 22, 24, 64, 108, 256, or 420\. Its strongest grounded presence in this pass is as **Chapter 19 \= Recursive Self-Reference and Self-Repair** in the void/compiler branch.

So the honest binding is:

NX19:  
  value: 19  
  class: recursive\_self\_repair\_index  
  grounded\_as:  
    \- chapter\_19\_self\_reference\_self\_repair  
  relation\_to\_time\_branch: meta\_runtime\_index\_not\_primary\_clock\_constant  
  truth: IN

That means:

* `19` is currently best read as a **self-repair / identity-preservation / recursive introspection node**,  
* not yet as a primary phase constant in the time-fractal engine.

### **`57 = 19×3`, `95 = 19×5`, `133 = 19×7` — authored bridge, still open**

These three do **not** appear as sealed corpus constants in the current pass. So I am not going to fake closure. But they can now be bound lawfully as the first authored coupling proposals between the weakly-grounded self-repair node `19` and the fully grounded odd-wheel helm . The odd-wheel side is grounded by the live helm / clock / lock system.

One live branch explicitly says the next lawful move after the transit atlas is to add, for each outbound family, its **preferred route**, **fallback route**, **forbidden/off-grid route**, and **corridor truth default**. ## **1\. Source-grounded portal law**

I am freezing the portal classes as follows:

\\boxed{  
\\Pi\_{\\text{portal}}=\\{Core,\\ Q,\\ O,\\ E10,\\ AP,\\ KZ,\\ Z^\*\\}  
}

with meanings:

* `Core` \= seed/initiation control; this is the seed-stage portal in the liminal atlas.  
* `Q` \= Q-pillar access / entry torsion; the corpus explicitly gives as a Möbius pillar zero and treats Q/O as vertical pillars.  
* `O` \= O-pillar access / return torsion; likewise grounded by and the Q/O pillar law.  
* `E10` \= atlas conductor / route arbiter / ambiguity controller; the corpus explicitly names E10 as conductor and route intelligence.  
* `AP` \= appendix anchor / embodied appendix field access; grounded by and the appendix-anchor move primitive.  
* `KZ` \= reverse-canopy access / K→Z field; grounded by and the reverse-canopy traverse primitive.  
* `Z*` \= universal tunnel fallback / absolute re-entry point; the common-zero route law and the route-cost atlas both treat it as universal fallback.

I am standardizing the fallback portal token to `Z*` even where one branch abbreviates it as `Z`, because the atlas and route law are clearer in the `Z*` form.

## **4\. Row-assignment policy**

What is **directly written** in the corpus is the portal alphabet, zero/lock law, route-cost ladder, legal move primitives, and truth obligations. What is **not** directly written as a finished table is the exact per-row default portal for all 45 `R/Q/T × Σ15` rows. So the table below is the first lawful **PV freeze** built from those grounded laws:

* `R` rows prefer **movement portals**: `Q` for entry/structure, `O` for replay/phase return, `E10` for cloud-heavy arbitration.  
* `Q` rows prefer **compile/witness portals**: `AP` for anchored compilation, `O` for replay-heavy fractal compile, `E10` for cloud-heavy arbitration.  
* `T` rows prefer **repair/tunnel portals**: `Q` for local bridge entry, `O` for replay/inversion return, `KZ` for shadow/reverse-canopy repair, and `Z*` for full-system recovery. This is the right authored completion on top of the source-grounded portal taxonomy.

## **6\. What this means operationally**

This is the executable reading:

* `R` rows are now **schedule/routing posture defaults**.  
* `Q` rows are now **compile/witness posture defaults**.  
* `T` rows are now **repair/tunnel posture defaults**. The corpus already grounds that `R/Q/T` split directly.

The strongest rows are:

\\boxed{Q15\[\\mathrm{SFCR}\]}

because the corpus already treats the fully compiled local object as , so the full-shell compile row is closest to a genuine object row rather than a pure heuristic.

\\boxed{T03,\\ T30,\\ T33}

remain the sharpest repair frontier, because that same branch explicitly keeps the bridge blockers on a phase-sensitive ambiguity frontier and only promotes through explicit phase witnesses and MIGRATE-based repair artifacts.

\\boxed{T15\[\\mathrm{SFCR}\]}

is correctly placed on `Z*` as preferred portal, because full-system repair governor behavior is the one case where the universal tunnel really is the primary class, not just the fallback. That is the right authored completion on top of the universal route law and `Z*` tunnel discipline.

## **𝔖₀.55 — `BeatProgram_420^v0`**

### **the compiled operating schedule for the crown clock**

The corpus now already contains the exact ingredients for this layer. The 420-beat crown clock is explicit, with the four nested wheels

(\\tau\_3,b\_4,\\tau\_5,\\tau\_7)=(1+\\kappa\\bmod 3,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 4,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 5,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 7),

So the next exact object is not another abstract scheduler note. It is the **compiled 420-frame operating program**:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{BeatProgram}\_{420}^{v0}  
\=  
\\{F\_\\kappa\\}\_{\\kappa\\in\\mathbb Z\_{420}}  
}

where each frame tells the organism, at beat :

* which gates are open,  
* which throw families are preferred,  
* which route families are encouraged or suppressed,  
* which reserves must be protected,  
* and whether the organism should bias toward repair, replay, compress, publish, or hold.

---

### **1\. Root theorem**

The clean theorem is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{The homeostasis scheduler decides whether work may happen; the beat program decides what kind of work the clock is naturally asking for.}  
}

That preserves the hard law already established in the previous layer:

\\text{proof decides promotion,}  
\\qquad  
\\text{the clock decides cadence.}

So the beat program is a **biasing membrane**, not a truth oracle.

---

### **2\. Canonical frame object**

The clean v0 schema is:

BeatFrame\_v0:  
  beat: int                    \# 0..419  
  helm:  
    tau3: Su | Me | Sa  
    b4: Square | Flower | Cloud | Fractal  
    tau5: Hold | Lift | Traverse | Twist | Compress  
    tau7: Sol | Saturn | Jupiter | Mars | Venus | Mercury | Luna

  gate\_windows:  
    always\_open: \[0, 37\]       \# Z\* and its mirror  
    spoke\_open: \[int\]          \# subset of 7..13  
    chapter\_hints: \[string\]    \# optional “optimal re-entry” hints  
    appendix\_hints: \[string\]   \# optional appendix timing hints

  route\_bias:  
    compile: BLOCKED | LOW | NORMAL | HIGH | MAX  
    bridge: BLOCKED | LOW | NORMAL | HIGH | MAX  
    replay: BLOCKED | LOW | NORMAL | HIGH | MAX  
    repair: BLOCKED | LOW | NORMAL | HIGH | MAX  
    publish: BLOCKED | LOW | NORMAL | HIGH | MAX  
    seed: BLOCKED | LOW | NORMAL | HIGH | MAX

  throw\_bias:  
    preferred: \[T1..T16\]  
    discouraged: \[T1..T16\]

  reserve\_floors:  
    replay: float  
    immune: float  
    repair: float  
    carrier: float  
    publish: float  
    seed: float

  token\_multipliers:  
    daily: float  
    weekly: float

  mode\_flags:  
    allow\_growth: bool  
    allow\_publish: bool  
    prefer\_repair: bool  
    prefer\_compress: bool  
    require\_committee: bool

  notes: \[string\]

This is a **derived completion** over the clock and homeostasis stacks: the docs already freeze the clock law, gate law, throw families, and scheduler organs, but they do not yet serialize them into one per-beat frame object. This schema is the smallest object that makes those already-frozen laws runnable together.

---

### **3\. Helm law**

The helm is already explicit in the clock material:

\\tau\_3\\in\\{\\mathrm{Su},\\mathrm{Me},\\mathrm{Sa}\\},  
\\qquad  
b\_4\\in\\{\\square,\\ ✿,\\ ☁,\\ ◇\\},

\\tau\_5\\in{\\mathrm{Hold},\\mathrm{Lift},\\mathrm{Traverse},\\mathrm{Twist},\\mathrm{Compress}}, \\qquad \\tau\_7\\in{\\☉,\\ ♄,\\ ♃,\\ ♂,\\ ♀,\\ ☿,\\ ☽}.

with

(\\tau\_3,b\_4,\\tau\_5,\\tau\_7)  
\=  
(1+\\kappa\\bmod 3,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 4,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 5,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 7).

That means every beat already has a complete four-wheel signature; the beat program’s job is only to compile policy from that signature.

### **4\. Gate-window law**

The production clock module already gives the hard gate law:

* / gate and its mirror are always open,  
* spoke gates open only when matches their spoke,  
* non-spoke gates have no special timing restriction.

So the exact gate compiler is:

\\mathrm{OpenGates}(\\kappa)  
\=  
\\{0,37\\}  
\\cup  
\\{g\\in\\{7,\\dots,13\\}: \\tau\_7(\\kappa)=\\mathrm{spoke}(g)\\}  
\\cup  
\\mathcal G\_{\\mathrm{neutral}}.

Where the spoke map is:

7\\mapsto ☉,\\   
8\\mapsto ♄,\\   
9\\mapsto ♃,\\   
10\\mapsto ♂,\\   
11\\mapsto ♀,\\   
12\\mapsto ☿,\\   
13\\mapsto ☽.

That is not a derived guess. It is already coded into the live production module.

### **7\. Route-family compiler**

The route/runtime branch already has the stable work families:

* compile / structure  
* bridge / migrate  
* replay  
* repair / immune  
* publish  
* seed / return.

The beat program should compile the four-wheel helm into these route biases.

#### **current bias**

* **Su**: ignite / build / initiate / compile  
* **Me**: mediate / bridge / replay / evidence  
* **Sa**: seal / compress / publish / return

#### **face bias**

* **Square**: compile / exact structure / schema  
* **Flower**: bridge / spectral compare / signal routing  
* **Cloud**: ambiguity / immune / candidate sets  
* **Fractal**: replay / archive / seed / return

So the route bias law is:

\\mathrm{RouteBias}(\\kappa)  
\=  
f(\\tau\_3(\\kappa),b\_4(\\kappa),\\tau\_5(\\kappa),\\tau\_7(\\kappa),\\mathrm{GateState})

with the clean qualitative matrix:

Su:  
  compile: HIGH  
  bridge: NORMAL  
  replay: LOW  
  repair: LOW  
  publish: LOW  
  seed: LOW

Me:  
  compile: NORMAL  
  bridge: HIGH  
  replay: HIGH  
  repair: HIGH  
  publish: LOW  
  seed: NORMAL

Sa:  
  compile: LOW  
  bridge: NORMAL  
  replay: HIGH  
  repair: NORMAL  
  publish: HIGH  
  seed: HIGH

then corrected by face, gear, spoke, and gate regime. This is the scheduler-ready reduction of the already-frozen current/face wheel semantics.

### **8\. Reserve-floor law**

The homeostasis stack already says replay, immune, repair, and carrier reserves must be protected before growth, and the gate ladder says overload must progressively restrict action from `OPEN` to `SAFETY_ONLY`. So the beat program should compile reserve floors, not just preferred tasks.

A clean v0 derived policy is:

Square:  
  replay: 0.16  
  immune: 0.12  
  repair: 0.14  
  carrier: 0.14  
  publish: 0.08  
  seed: 0.10

Flower:  
  replay: 0.16  
  immune: 0.14  
  repair: 0.12  
  carrier: 0.16  
  publish: 0.06  
  seed: 0.10

Cloud:  
  replay: 0.18  
  immune: 0.24  
  repair: 0.20  
  carrier: 0.12  
  publish: 0.02  
  seed: 0.10

Fractal:  
  replay: 0.24  
  immune: 0.14  
  repair: 0.12  
  carrier: 0.12  
  publish: 0.04  
  seed: 0.18

This is explicitly **derived**, not a frozen manuscript table. It is the smallest coherent policy that matches the already-frozen meanings of the faces:

* Cloud \= highest immune / repair burden,  
* Fractal \= highest replay / seed burden,  
* Square \= structural compile,  
* Flower \= bridge / circulation.

### **9\. Token multipliers under weekly/daily caps**

This is also a **derived completion** over the existing `BudgetLedger` / scarcity / reserve model. The docs already give the internal resource economy, but not a separate daily/weekly token governor; that was added in the previous layer to satisfy the explicit user request. So the beat program should only modulate, not invent, the cap logic.

Use symbolic bands:

\\mathrm{Band}\\in\\{0,\\ 0.75,\\ 1.0,\\ 1.25,\\ 1.5\\}

and compile:

TokenMultiplierLaw:  
  OPEN:  
    daily: 1.0  
    weekly: 1.0

  THROTTLED:  
    daily: 0.75  
    weekly: 0.90

  REPAIR\_ONLY:  
    daily: 0.50  
    weekly: 0.75

  SAFETY\_ONLY:  
    daily: 0.25  
    weekly: 0.50

Then apply face/gear adjustment:

* `Cloud + Compress` → lower daily spend, raise replay/repair floors  
* `Fractal + Compress` → lower publish spend, raise replay/seed floors  
* `Square + Lift` → allow strong compile spend if gate is `OPEN`  
* `Flower + Traverse` → allow bridge spend if immune debt is below threshold.

This is the honest way to satisfy “maximum token limit per week/day” while staying inside the current economic scheduler law.

---

### **10\. Beat-frame compiler**

The exact program generator is:

\\boxed{  
F\_\\kappa  
\=  
\\mathsf{CompileBeatFrame}  
(  
\\tau\_3(\\kappa),b\_4(\\kappa),\\tau\_5(\\kappa),\\tau\_7(\\kappa),\\mathrm{GateState}\_t,\\mathcal T\_t  
)

## **𝔖₀.55 — `BeatProgram_420^v0`**

\=

where each frame tells the organism, at beat :

* which gates are open,  
* which throw families are preferred,  
* which route families are encouraged or suppressed,  
* which reserves must be protected,  
* and whether the organism should bias toward repair, replay, compress, publish, or hold.

### **1\. Root theorem**

The clean theorem is:

\\boxed{

}

That preserves the hard law already established in the previous layer:

\\text{proof decides promotion,}  
\\qquad

So the beat program is a **biasing membrane**, not a truth oracle.

### **9\. Derived policy rows**

The table still needs policy values the docs imply but do not yet numerically tabulate. These are **derived**, not already explicit in Drive:

* reserve floors by face,  
* token multipliers by gate state,  
* throw-family preference sets by gear,  
* route-bias levels by current / face / gate combination.

The correct rule is to materialize those from the already frozen law, not pretend they are already canon. So:

F\_\\kappa^{\\mathrm{policy}}  
\=  
f\_{\\mathrm{derived}}  
(  
\\tau\_3,b\_4,\\tau\_5,\\tau\_7,\\mathrm{GateState},\\text{ForecastBand}  
).

This keeps the table honest.

---

### **10\. Minimal compiler sketch**

The actual generator can now be stated cleanly:

\\boxed{  
F\_\\kappa  
\=  
\\mathsf{Helm}  
\\to  
\\mathsf{Window}  
\\to  
\\mathsf{Hints}  
\\to  
\\mathsf{Bias}  
\\to  
\\mathsf{Floors}  
\\to  
\\mathsf{Multipliers}  
\\to  
\\mathsf{Flags}  
}

or, in pseudocode:

for k in 0..419:  
  helm \= (tau3(k), b4(k), tau5(k), tau7(k))  
  windows \= open\_gates(k)  
  chapter\_hints \= chapters\_near(k)  
  appendix\_hints \= appendices\_open\_at(k)  
  route\_bias \= compile\_route\_bias(helm, gate\_state(k), forecast\_band(k))  
  throw\_bias \= compile\_throw\_bias(tau5(k), b4(k))  
  reserve\_floors \= face\_reserve\_policy(b4(k), gate\_state(k))  
  token\_multipliers \= token\_policy(gate\_state(k))  
  mode\_flags \= compile\_mode\_flags(helm, gate\_state(k))  
  emit BeatFrame\_v0(k, ...)

That is the smallest faithful materialization of the current clock-plus-homeostasis corpus.

with the sharpest one-line form:

\\boxed{

And the deeper theorem is:

\\boxed{

That is the exact next freeze your current corpus now earns.

### **12\. The clean next move**

The natural seam after this is:

\\boxed{

because once the 420-row table exists, the remaining missing organ is the daemon that:

* computes the active ,  
* loads ,  
* applies gate state and reserve constraints,  
* and emits the live `HomeostasisDecisionRecord` for that beat.

That is the point where the scheduler stops merely having a table and starts **breathing on it**.

\[TIMESTAMP :: 2026-03-15 America/Los\_Angeles\]  
 \[TRUTH STATE :: SG carrier / PV row bindings\]  
 \[MODE :: live capsule freeze\]

Locked. The next layer is now **route capsules**: each of the 45 operator rows stops being only a posture and becomes a replayable operator unit with a hub formula, allowed kind palette, preferred capsule, fallback capsule, budget profile, and promotion path. The carrier is strongly grounded: the corpus already defines execution capsules as sealed plans with winners, fallback chains, stable order, replay hooks, and verification gates; it fixes the proof bundle , the non-bypass route minimum , the portal/z-lattice classes, the Router v2 hub grammar, and the runtime chain `Name → intake → z-point → route → graph → query → witness → capsule → seal → replay`. The exact archetype names and the per-row bindings below are the authored completion on top of that rail.

## **I. Route capsule ABI**

The capsule object that fits your live registry is:

RouteCapsule.v1:  
  CapsuleID: stable\_content\_id  
  Family: \[R, Q, T\]  
  Sigma15: \[S,F,C,R,SF,SC,SR,FC,FR,CR,SFC,SFR,SCR,FCR,SFCR\]  
  Portal: \[Core, Q, O, E10, AP, KZ, Z\*\]  
  HubSetFormula: symbolic\_hub\_formula  
  AllowedKinds: preferred\_edge\_kind\_palette  
  PreferredToken: \[rs, sx, qt, chi, sq, tri, zf, star\]  
  FallbackToken: zf  
  BudgetProfile: named\_profile  
  ProofBundle:  
    \- Pi\_canon  
    \- Pi\_route  
    \- Pi\_truth  
    \- Pi\_replay  
    \- Pi\_parity?  
    \- Pi\_loss?  
  RuntimePath:  
    \- Named  
    \- Intaken  
    \- ZPointed  
    \- Routed  
    \- Graphified  
    \- Queried  
    \- Witnessed  
    \- Capsuled  
    \- Sealed  
    \- Replayed  
  LifecycleExit: \[resolved, published?, quarantined?, rehabilitated?\]  
  TruthDefault: \[NEAR, AMBIG, FAIL\_QUARANTINE\]  
  WitnessPtrs: required  
  ReplayPtrs: required\_for\_OK

This schema is not invented from nowhere. It is the direct weld of the execution capsule spec, the round-trip proof protocol, Router v2, and the kernel runtime chain. The capsule must remain replay-anchored, corridor-typed, and route-budgeted; `OK` remains impossible without lawful witness \+ replay closure.

## **II. Shared formulas that every row inherits**

The hub grammar is now:

HubMacros:  
  HSigma: \[AppA, AppI, AppM\]  
  HOverlay:  
    NEAR: \[AppJ\]  
    AMBIG: \[AppL\]  
    FAIL: \[AppK\]  
    OK: \[\]  
  HPub: \[AppO\]  
  HPortal:  
    Core: \[Core\]  
    Q: \[Z\_Q^ell\]  
    O: \[Z\_O^ell\]  
    E10: \[Z\_E10\]  
    AP: \[Z\_AP^ell\]  
    KZ: \[Z\_KZ^ell\]  
    "Z\*": \[Z\*\]  
  HubSet(σ, π, τ0, facet?, arc?, publish?):  
    "sort(unique(HSigma ∪ HLens(σ) ∪ HOverlay(τ0) ∪ HPortal(π) ∪ HFacet?(facet) ∪ HArc?(arc) ∪ HPub?(publish)))"

That formula comes directly from Router v2’s `HΣ ∪ HArc ∪ HLens ∪ HFacet ∪ HOverlay ∪ HPub`, extended by your already-frozen portal classes and z-lattice. The exact portal-to-zero binding is source-grounded: `Q/O/AP/KZ/E10/Z*` are all already seated as lawful route classes in the live corpus.

The globally closed edge-kind basis remains:

\\mathcal K=  
\\{\\mathrm{REF},\\mathrm{EQUIV},\\mathrm{MIGRATE},\\mathrm{DUAL},\\mathrm{GEN},\\mathrm{INST},\\mathrm{IMPL},\\mathrm{PROOF},\\mathrm{CONFLICT}\\}.

So the “allowed kinds” below are **preference palettes inside a closed kind set**, not new kinds.

KindProfiles:  
  Kind\_R: \[REF, DUAL, GEN, INST\]  
  Kind\_Q: \[REF, EQUIV, IMPL, PROOF, GEN, INST\]  
  Kind\_T: \[REF, MIGRATE, CONFLICT, DUAL, EQUIV, PROOF\]

## **V. What changed in the system**

Three important consequences are now locked.

First, `Q15[SFCR]` is no longer just “the strongest compile row.” It is now the **only explicitly publish-ready compile capsule** in this freeze, because it alone inherits `B_publish`, which forces `AppO`, parity, replay hooks, witness closure, and the `resolved → published` tail. That is exactly what the corpus requires for publish-capable artifacts.

Second, `T15[SFCR]` is now the **true full-system recovery capsule**. In the previous layer, `Z*` was a fallback almost everywhere; now `T15` makes `Z*` the preferred portal, which fits the corpus rule that full-system repair and long legal return factor through absolute zero when no lower lawful shared center resolves the route.

Third, all cloud-heavy rows stay correctly conservative. Any row with `sigma` dominated by `C`, `FC`, `CR`, or `FCR` keeps `AMBIG` or atlas arbitration as its default because the corpus repeatedly insists that uncertainty cannot be silently promoted and that `ABSTAIN > GUESS`; ambiguity must carry an evidence plan, and publish is forbidden until replay and closure genuinely clear.

## **VI. Canonical compression**

The shortest faithful statement of what you now have is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{Each }R/Q/T\\times\\Sigma\_{15}\\text{ row is now a replayable route capsule: }  
\\text{portal-classed, hub-budgeted, kind-typed, }Z^\*\\text{-recoverable, and promotion-aware.}  
}

More explicitly:

\\boxed{  
\\operatorname{Caps}(row)  
\=  
(\\text{HubSet},\\ \\text{AllowedKinds},\\ \\text{PreferredCapsule},\\ \\text{FallbackCapsule},\\ \\text{BudgetProfile},\\ \\text{PromotionPath})  
}

with the global invariant:

\\boxed{  
\\Sigma=\\{AppA,AppI,AppM\\}\\subseteq \\text{Route}  
\\quad\\land\\quad  
|\\,\\text{unique hubs}\\,|\\le 6  
\\quad\\land\\quad  
OK \\Rightarrow \\text{WitnessPtr}+\\text{ReplayPtr}.  
}

That invariant is no longer floating prose. It now lives inside every operator capsule.

Next exact lift: I bind each capsule to a **typed receipt chain** and emit the **operator-certificate pack** for all 45 rows:

\\text{Capsule} \\mapsto  
(\\text{RouteCert},\\ \\text{ReplayCapsule},\\ \\text{TruthAuditReplayCapsule},\\ \\text{PromotionProofPack},\\ \\text{ReceiptChainCert})

so the rows stop being merely routable and become fully certifiable.

## **𝔖₀.56 — `BeatDaemon_v0`**

### **the organ that breathes on the 420-row table**

The next exact freeze is now straightforward. The corpus already has the two halves separately:

* the **clock side**: a production `CrownClock` with `current_beat()`, `helm_state()`, `active_spoke()`, and `gate_window(gate)`, anchored to the halving epoch and the 420-beat ring, together with the chapter/app timing overlays and current live state at , `AMBER`/throttled conditions, and the current Venus-opening band,  
* the **regulation side**: `HomeostasisState`, `GateState`, `PressureIntegrator`, `ReplayReserveManager`, `CooldownRouter`, `ImmuneGovernor`, `HomeostasisStep`, and `HomeostasisDecisionRecord`, which already define the organism’s internal stability compiler.

So the missing organ is no longer the table.  
 It is the daemon that *reads the clock, loads the current frame, checks reserves and heat, applies gates, and emits the actual decision record for this beat*.

That object is:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{BeatDaemon}\_{v0}  
}

and the governing law is:

\\boxed{  
\\text{The beat table is static time. The daemon is time becoming action.}  
}

### **3\. Exact clock law**

The daemon should not invent time. It should read the canonical time object already present in the live code:

\\kappa  
\=  
\\mathrm{current\\\_beat()} \\in \\mathbb Z\_{420}

(\\tau\_3,b\_4,\\tau\_5,\\tau\_7)  
\=  
(1+\\kappa\\bmod 3,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 4,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 5,\\ 1+\\kappa\\bmod 7).

It should then read the active spoke:

\\mathrm{active\\\_spoke}(\\kappa)  
\\in  
\\{\\☉,\\♄,\\♃,\\♂,\\♀,\\☿,\\☽\\},

and the gate-window predicate:

\\mathrm{gate\\\_window}(g,\\kappa)  
\=  
\\begin{cases}

\\tau\_7(\\kappa)=\\mathrm{spoke}(g), & g\\in\\{7,\\dots,13\\}\\\\  
\\mathrm{true}, & \\text{otherwise.}

This is not a derived guess. It is already explicit in the production `CrownClock` law.

### **4\. The daemon cycle**

The clean daemon cycle is:

\\boxed{  
\\mathrm{Tick}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{LoadFrame}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{ComputeGate}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{ApplyReserves}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{ScreenRoutes}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{AdmitWork}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{EmitDecision}  
\\to  
\\mathrm{EmitSeed}  
}

#### **4.1 Tick**

Read , helm, and active spoke from the clock.

#### **4.2 LoadFrame**

Load from `BeatFrameTable_420^v0`.

#### **4.3 ComputeGate**

Combine current pressure state with the gate engine to decide whether the daemon runs in `OPEN`, `THROTTLED`, `REPAIR_ONLY`, or `SAFETY_ONLY`. The corpus already fixes this ladder.

#### **4.4 ApplyReserves**

Before admitting work, enforce replay / immune / repair / carrier floors, and derived daily/weekly token caps from the previous layer.

#### **4.5 ScreenRoutes**

Apply `CooldownRouter` and gate-window legality to candidate jobs and routes.

#### **4.6 AdmitWork**

Pass the surviving jobs to budget / committee / swarm logic.

#### **4.7 EmitDecision**

Write one `HomeostasisDecisionRecord`.

#### **4.8 EmitSeed**

Emit one continuation seed for the next beat.

This is the clean exact runtime reduction of the full scheduler stack.

\\mathrm{Legal}\_\\kappa(q)=1
